Total number of release-critical bugs: 2103
Number that have a patch: 433

Number that are being ignored: 29
Number concerning the current stable release: 1274
Number concerning the next release: 831

Explanation for bug
tags:


   P: pending
   +: patch
   H: help
   M: moreinfo
   R: unreproducible
   S: security
   U: upstream
   I: lenny-ignore or squeeze-ignore



The second set of tags indicate what releases a bug applies to:
O for oldstable (sarge), S for stable (lenny), T for testing (squeeze),
U for unstable (sid) or E for experimental.
